<Text>I heard they had the best falafel on the west coast and my god they were amazing. Crispy on the outside and perfect wet texture on the inside. They were super flavorful and so savory.

The Moroccan cigars you can tell are home made and made with love. These are not frozen from restaurant depot. Each is hand rolled and stuffed with meaty goodness.

Hummus was fresh and perfectly spiced. The pita were also warm, fluffy and toasted to perfection.

If you are down for some Cholent or Jachnun - both Shabbat delicacies. Then come on Sunday and these items are LIT.

Their grilled chicken plate was super flavorful and just so fresh and light. I can eat that all day.

The ambiance is fresh, airy and most importantly CLEAN. I met the owners, a very sweet and welcoming Israeli woman and her Moroccan husband. You get the feeling they transported their home countries to the Valley and all of the hospitality, flavors, and dishes are made with that purpose.

Would go again!

P.S. the pickled veggie bar, the home made olives, the nana tea, the Turkish coffee, the baklava bites, the cabbage salad... all spot on.<//Text><Pics>None</Pics></record></dataset><record>

< review>
Joy and her team were on time, personable, knowledgeable and encouraging. She and her assistant guided us as a group, but also one-on-one tips as we experience painting challenges. They brought their own music that help create an atmosphere of togetherness. Joy's analogy for each brush and stroke ability still remains with me today, very useful. I really appreciated that the brushes were in good condition, not overly worn out with stray bristles pointing in different direction which tend to mess up your picture. She had good smooth bristle brushes. I will definitely use the services of Joyful Expression again.</review>
